============================================================
SNAPSHOT IGNORE POLICY
============================================================

This file is rebuilt from the current Portfolio workspace every time ./read_project.sh runs.
Ignored paths are omitted from the project tree and file dumps unless they appear inside an included text file such as .gitignore or read_project.sh.

The snapshot intentionally ignores generated/cache/runtime/private files:
- .git
- node_modules
- .next
- out
- dist
- build
- .cache
- .turbo
- .npm
- .pnpm-store
- .yarn
- .DS_Store
- next-env.d.ts
- *.tsbuildinfo
- *_PROJECT_SNAPSHOT.txt
- *.zip
- .env and .env*.local

Binary image, PDF, and archive files are inventoried by path, size, and modified time only. Raw binary bytes are not printed.

   356	function PhonePreview({
   357	  title,
   358	  metric,
   359	  variant,
   360	  href,
   361	  screenImageSrc,
   362	  screenImageAlt,
   363	}: {
   364	  href?: string;
   365	  title: string;
   366	  metric: string;
   367	  variant: "commerce" | "finance";
   368	  screenImageSrc?: string;
   369	  screenImageAlt?: string;
   370	}) {
   371	  const className = `phone-shell phone-shell-${variant}${
   372	    screenImageSrc ? " phone-shell-capture" : ""
   373	  }${href ? " phone-shell-link" : ""}`;
   374	  const content = (
   375	    <>
   376	      <div className="phone-speaker" />
   377	      <div className={`phone-screen${screenImageSrc ? " has-image" : ""}`}>
   378	        {screenImageSrc ? (
   379	          <div className="phone-screen-image-frame">
   380	            <Image
   381	              alt={screenImageAlt ?? `${title} app screen`}
   382	              className="phone-screen-image"
   383	              fill
   384	              sizes="245px"
   385	              src={screenImageSrc}
   386	            />
   387	          </div>
   388	        ) : (
   389	          <>
   390	            <div className="phone-status">
   391	              <span>{title}</span>
   392	              <span>5G</span>
   393	            </div>
   394	            <div className="phone-chart">
   395	              <div />
   396	              <div />
   397	              <div />
   398	              <div />
   399	            </div>
   400	            <div className="phone-cardline wide" />
   401	            <div className="phone-cardline" />
   402	            <div className="phone-grid">
   403	              <span />
   404	              <span />
   405	              <span />
   406	              <span />
   407	            </div>
   408	            <div className="phone-cta">{metric}</div>
   409	          </>
   410	        )}
   411	      </div>
   412	    </>
   413	  );
   414	
   415	  if (href) {
   416	    return (
   417	      <a
   418	        aria-label={`Open ${title} case study`}
   419	        className={className}
   420	        href={href}
   421	      >
   422	        {content}
   423	      </a>
   424	    );
   425	  }
   426	
   427	  return <div className={className}>{content}</div>;
   428	}

   463	function CaseStudyTitle({ study }: { study: CaseStudy }) {
   464	  const variant = caseTitleVariants[study.id];
   465	
   466	  if (study.id === "this-portfolio-website") {
   467	    return (
   468	      <h3 className="case-card-title-stack" aria-label={study.title}>
   469	        <span className="case-card-project-title-name-stack case-card-portfolio-title-stack">
   470	          <span className="case-card-title-underline">Prahl.dev</span>
   471	          <span className="case-card-title-website-label">(THIS WEBSITE)</span>
   472	        </span>

   474	          <ProjectDeviceStack
   475	            assetGap="0.42em"
   476	            color="#ffb866"
   477	            hasWeb
   478	            mobilePlatforms={[]}
   479	            responsiveAssetGap={caseTitleDeviceGap}
   480	            webIconScale={caseTitleMatchedWebIconScale}
   481	          />
   482	        </span>
   483	      </h3>
   484	    );
   485	  }
   486	
   487	  if (!variant) {
   488	    return <h3>{study.title}</h3>;
   489	  }
   490

   494	        className="case-card-project-title-name-stack"

   506	          paintOrder: "stroke fill",

   523	          assetGap="0.42em"
   524	          color={variant.color}
   525	          hasTablet={variant.hasTablet}

   528	          responsiveAssetGap={caseTitleDeviceGap}
   529	          webIconScale={variant.webIconScale}
   530	        />
   531	      </span>
   532	    </h3>
   533	  );
   534	}

   536	function CaseStudyCard({ study }: { study: CaseStudy }) {
   537	  const usesLandscapeLayout =
   538	    study.screenshots.length === 1 &&
   539	    study.screenshots[0]?.orientation === "landscape";
   540	  const usesPairLayout = study.screenshots.length === 2;
   541	  const description = study.descriptionLines.join(" ");
   542	  const eyebrow = study.eyebrowLines.join(" ");
   543	  const content = (
   544	    <>
   545	      <div className="case-topline">
   546	        <CaseEyebrow label={eyebrow} />
   547	        <div className="case-stat-stack">
   548	          <strong>{study.stat}</strong>
   549	          <span className="case-worklog-stat">{study.worklogStat}</span>
   550	        </div>
   551	      </div>
   552	      <CaseStudyTitle study={study} />
   553	      <CaseDescription label={description} lines={study.descriptionLines} />
   554	      <div className="case-tags">
   555	        {study.tags.map((tag) => (
   556	          <span key={tag}>{tag}</span>
   557	        ))}
   558	      </div>
   559	      {study.screenshots.length > 0 ? (
   560	        <div
   561	          aria-label={`${study.title} app screenshots`}
   562	          className={`case-miniatures${
   563	            usesLandscapeLayout ? " case-miniatures-landscape" : ""
   564	          }${usesPairLayout ? " case-miniatures-pair" : ""}`}
   565	        >
   566	          {study.screenshots.map((screenshot) => (
   567	            <Image
   568	              alt={screenshot.alt}
   569	              className={`case-miniature${
   570	                screenshot.orientation === "landscape"
   571	                  ? " case-miniature-landscape"
   572	                  : ""
   573	              }`}
   574	              height={screenshot.orientation === "landscape" ? 166 : 192}
   575	              key={screenshot.src}
   576	              src={screenshot.src}
   577	              width={screenshot.orientation === "landscape" ? 238 : 108}
   578	            />
   579	          ))}
   580	        </div>
   581	      ) : null}
   582	    </>
   583	  );
   584	
   585	  if (study.href) {
   586	    return (
   587	      <a
   588	        aria-label={`Open ${study.title} case study`}
   589	        className="case-card case-card-link"
   590	        href={study.href}
   591	        id={study.id}
   592	      >
   593	        {content}
   594	      </a>
   595	    );
   596	  }
   597	
   598	  return (
   599	    <article className="case-card" id={study.id}>
   600	      {content}
   601	    </article>
   602	  );
   603	}

    74	function getCaseStudyRowScrollOffset() {
    75	  const isWideLandscape = window.matchMedia(
    76	    "(min-width: 1024px) and (orientation: landscape)",
    77	  ).matches;
    78	  const isPortrait = window.matchMedia("(orientation: portrait)").matches;
    79	
    80	  if (isWideLandscape) {
    81	    return Math.max(18, Math.min(44, window.innerHeight * 0.035));
    82	  }
    83	
    84	  if (isPortrait) {
    85	    return Math.max(14, Math.min(36, window.innerHeight * 0.03));
    86	  }
    87	
    88	  return Math.max(16, Math.min(40, window.innerHeight * 0.0325));
    89	}
    90	
    91	function scrollCaseStudyRowIntoView(caseStudyId: string) {
    92	  const targetCard = document.getElementById(caseStudyId);
    93	
    94	  if (!targetCard) {
    95	    return;
    96	  }
    97	
    98	  const caseGrid = targetCard.closest<HTMLElement>(".case-grid");
    99	  const targetTop = targetCard.getBoundingClientRect().top;
   100	  const rowCards = caseGrid
   101	    ? Array.from(caseGrid.children).filter((child): child is HTMLElement => {
   102	        if (!(child instanceof HTMLElement)) {
   103	          return false;
   104	        }
   105	
   106	        const cardTop = child.getBoundingClientRect().top;
   107	
   108	        return Math.abs(cardTop - targetTop) <= 8;
   109	      })
   110	    : [targetCard];
   111	  const rowTop = Math.min(
   112	    ...rowCards.map((card) => card.getBoundingClientRect().top),
   113	  );
   114	
   115	  window.scrollTo({
   116	    behavior: "smooth",
   117	    top: window.scrollY + rowTop - getCaseStudyRowScrollOffset(),
   118	  });
   119	
   120	  window.history.replaceState(null, "", `#${caseStudyId}`);
   121	}
   122	
   123	const androidLogoSize = {
   124	  height: 8.69299,
   125	  width: 10.86624,
   126	};
   127	
   128	const iosLogoSize = {
   129	  height: 10.47816,
   130	  width: 10.47816,
   131	};

   133	function AndroidLogoImage({ x, y }: { x: number; y: number }) {
   134	  return (
   135	    <image
   136	      height={androidLogoSize.height}
   137	      href="/images/android-device-logo.svg"
   138	      preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet"
   139	      width={androidLogoSize.width}
   140	      x={x}
   141	      y={y}
   142	    />
   143	  );
   144	}
   145	
   146	function PhoneAndroidIcon({ slot }: { slot: "single" | "top" }) {
   147	  const y = slot === "single" ? 11.43286 : 6.93286;
   148	
   149	  return <AndroidLogoImage x={6.23608} y={y} />;
   150	}

   152	function IosLogoImage({ x, y }: { x: number; y: number }) {
   153	  return (
   154	    <image
   155	      height={iosLogoSize.height}
   156	      href="/images/ios-device-logo.svg"
   157	      preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet"
   158	      width={iosLogoSize.width}
   159	      x={x}
   160	      y={y}
   161	    />
   162	  );
   163	}
   164	
   165	function PhoneAppleIcon({ slot }: { slot: "bottom" | "single" }) {
   166	  const y = slot === "single" ? 11.27372 : 17.47372;
   167	
   168	  return <IosLogoImage x={5.92372} y={y} />;
   169	}

   171	function PhoneMark({
   172	  mobilePlatforms,
   173	}: {
   174	  mobilePlatforms: MobilePlatform[];
   175	}) {
   176	  return (
   177	    <svg
   178	      aria-hidden
   179	      className="carousel-button-phone"
   180	      height="1.936em"
   181	      style={{ height: "1.936em", width: "1.36125em" }}
   182	      viewBox="0 0 22.5 32"
   183	      width="1.36125em"
   184	    >
   185	      <rect
   186	        className="phone-mini-frame"
   187	        height="29.2"
   188	        rx="2.7"
   189	        width="19"
   190	        x="1.75"
   191	        y="1.4"
   192	      />
   193	      <rect
   194	        className="phone-mini-screen"
   195	        height="22.8"
   196	        rx="1.4"
   197	        width="14.5"
   198	        x="4"
   199	        y="4.6"
   200	      />
   201	      <path className="phone-mini-speaker" d="M8.875 3.2h4.75" />
   202	      <circle className="phone-mini-home" cx="11.25" cy="29" r="0.7" />
   203	      {mobilePlatforms.map((platform, index) => {
   204	        const slot =
   205	          mobilePlatforms.length === 1
   206	            ? "single"
   207	            : index === 0
   208	              ? "top"
   209	              : "bottom";
   210	
   211	        return platform === "android" ? (
   212	          <PhoneAndroidIcon
   213	            key={platform}
   214	            slot={slot === "bottom" ? "top" : slot}
   215	          />
   216	        ) : (
   217	          <PhoneAppleIcon
   218	            key={platform}
   219	            slot={slot === "top" ? "bottom" : slot}
   220	          />
   221	        );
   222	      })}
   223	    </svg>
   224	  );
   225	}

   271	function WebMark({ scale = 1 }: { scale?: number }) {
   272	  const size = `${(1.2 * scale).toFixed(3)}em`;
   273	
   274	  return (
   275	    <svg
   276	      aria-hidden
   277	      className="carousel-button-web"
   278	      height={size}
   279	      style={{ height: size, width: size }}
   280	      viewBox="0 0 24 24"
   281	      width={size}
   282	    >
   283	      <circle className="web-globe-shell" cx="12" cy="12" r="8.2" />
   284	      <path className="web-globe-line" d="M3.8 12h16.4" />
   285	      <path className="web-globe-line" d="M5.6 8.1h12.8" />
   286	      <path className="web-globe-line" d="M5.6 15.9h12.8" />
   287	      <path className="web-globe-line" d="M12 3.8c2.2 2.3 3.3 5 3.3 8.2s-1.1 5.9-3.3 8.2" />
   288	      <path className="web-globe-line" d="M12 3.8c-2.2 2.3-3.3 5-3.3 8.2s1.1 5.9 3.3 8.2" />
   289	    </svg>
   290	  );
   291	}
   292	
   293	export function ProjectDeviceStack({
   294	  assetGap,
   295	  color,
   296	  hasTablet,
   297	  hasWeb,
   298	  mobilePlatforms,
   299	  responsiveAssetGap,
   300	  webIconScale,
   301	}: {
   302	  assetGap?: string;
   303	  color: string;
   304	  hasTablet?: boolean;
   305	  hasWeb?: boolean;
   306	  mobilePlatforms: MobilePlatform[];
   307	  responsiveAssetGap?: ResponsiveAssetGap;
   308	  webIconScale?: number;
   309	}) {
   310	  const stackRef = useRef<HTMLSpanElement>(null);
   311	  const [measuredAssetGap, setMeasuredAssetGap] = useState<string | null>(null);
   312	  const stackStyle: CSSProperties & {
   313	    "--project-device-stack-gap"?: string;
   314	  } = {
   315	    color,
   316	  };
   317	  const stackGap = measuredAssetGap ?? assetGap;
   318	
   319	  useLayoutEffect(() => {
   320	    if (!responsiveAssetGap) {
   321	      setMeasuredAssetGap(null);
   322	      return;
   323	    }
   324	
   325	    const stack = stackRef.current;
   326	    const measurementTarget = stack?.parentElement ?? stack;
   327	
   328	    if (!measurementTarget) {
   329	      return;
   330	    }
   331	
   332	    let frame = 0;
   333	    const updateGap = () => {
   334	      if (frame) {
   335	        window.cancelAnimationFrame(frame);
   336	      }
   337	
   338	      frame = window.requestAnimationFrame(() => {
   339	        const laneWidth = measurementTarget.getBoundingClientRect().width;
   340	        const activeRange = Math.max(
   341	          1,
   342	          responsiveAssetGap.wideLanePx - responsiveAssetGap.tightLanePx,
   343	        );
   344	        const progress = Math.min(
   345	          1,
   346	          Math.max(
   347	            0,
   348	            (laneWidth - responsiveAssetGap.tightLanePx) / activeRange,
   349	          ),
   350	        );
   351	        const nextGap =
   352	          responsiveAssetGap.minPx +
   353	          (responsiveAssetGap.maxPx - responsiveAssetGap.minPx) * progress;
   354	        const nextGapValue = `${nextGap.toFixed(2)}px`;
   355	
   356	        setMeasuredAssetGap((currentGap) =>
   357	          currentGap === nextGapValue ? currentGap : nextGapValue,
   358	        );
   359	      });
   360	    };
   361	
   362	    updateGap();
   363	
   364	    const resizeObserver =
   365	      typeof ResizeObserver === "undefined"
   366	        ? null
   367	        : new ResizeObserver(updateGap);
   368	
   369	    resizeObserver?.observe(measurementTarget);
   370	    window.addEventListener("resize", updateGap);
   371	
   372	    return () => {
   373	      if (frame) {
   374	        window.cancelAnimationFrame(frame);
   375	      }
   376	
   377	      resizeObserver?.disconnect();
   378	      window.removeEventListener("resize", updateGap);
   379	    };
   380	  }, [
   381	    responsiveAssetGap?.maxPx,
   382	    responsiveAssetGap?.minPx,
   383	    responsiveAssetGap?.tightLanePx,
   384	    responsiveAssetGap?.wideLanePx,
   385	  ]);
   386	
   387	  if (stackGap) {
   388	    stackStyle["--project-device-stack-gap"] = stackGap;
   389	  }
   390	
   391	  return (
   392	    <span className="carousel-button-project" ref={stackRef} style={stackStyle}>
   393	      {mobilePlatforms.map((platform) => (
   394	        <PhoneMark key={platform} mobilePlatforms={[platform]} />
   395	      ))}
   396	      {hasTablet ? <TabletMark /> : null}
   397	      {hasWeb ? <WebMark scale={webIconScale} /> : null}
   398	    </span>
   399	  );
   400	}
   401	
   402	function CarouselArrowMark() {
   403	  return (
   404	    <img
   405	      alt=""
   406	      aria-hidden
   407	      className="carousel-button-arrow-mark"
   408	      draggable={false}
   409	      style={{
   410	        display: "block",
   411	        height: "100%",
   412	        verticalAlign: "top",
   413	        width: "100%",
   414	      }}
   415	      src="/images/carousel-arrow.svg"
   416	    />
   417	  );
   418	}
   419	
   420	export function ProjectCarouselButton() {
   421	  const [activeIndex, setActiveIndex] = useState(0);
   422	  const projectButtonRef = useRef<HTMLAnchorElement>(null);
   423	  const activeProject = projectLinks[activeIndex];
   424	
   425	  const handleArrowClick = (event: MouseEvent<HTMLAnchorElement>) => {
   426	    event.preventDefault();
   427	    scrollCaseStudyRowIntoView(activeProject.caseStudyId);
   428	  };
   429	
   430	  useEffect(() => {
   431	    const interval = window.setInterval(() => {
   432	      setActiveIndex((currentIndex) => (currentIndex + 1) % projectLinks.length);
   433	    }, 5000);
   434	
   435	    return () => window.clearInterval(interval);
   436	  }, []);
   437	
   438	  useLayoutEffect(() => {
   439	    let frame = 0;
   440	
   441	    const syncHeroActionGeometry = () => {
   442	      if (frame) {
   443	        window.cancelAnimationFrame(frame);
   444	      }
   445	
   446	      frame = window.requestAnimationFrame(() => {
   447	        const heroCopy = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>(".hero-copy");
   448	        const heroActions =
   449	          document.querySelector<HTMLElement>(".hero-actions");
   450	        const proofPanel = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>(".proof-panel");
   451	        const profilePhoto =
   452	          document.querySelector<HTMLElement>(".profile-photo");
   453	        const socialButton =
   454	          document.querySelector<HTMLElement>(".hero-social-button");
   455	
   456	        if (proofPanel && profilePhoto) {
   457	          const proofRect = proofPanel.getBoundingClientRect();
   458	          const profileRect = profilePhoto.getBoundingClientRect();
   459	          const proofWidth = profileRect.right - proofRect.left;
   460	
   461	          if (proofWidth > 0) {
   462	            proofPanel.style.setProperty(
   463	              "--hero-proof-landscape-width",
   464	              `${proofWidth}px`,
   465	            );
   466	          }
   467	        }
   468	
   469	        if (heroActions && socialButton) {
   470	          const heroActionsWidth = heroActions.getBoundingClientRect().width;
   471	          const socialButtonHeight =
   472	            socialButton.getBoundingClientRect().height;
   473	
   474	          if (heroCopy && heroActionsWidth > 0) {
   475	            heroCopy.style.setProperty(
   476	              "--hero-text-stack-width",
   477	              `${heroActionsWidth}px`,
   478	            );
   479	          }
   480	
   481	          if (socialButtonHeight > 0) {
   482	            const setPx = (name: string, value: number) => {
   483	              heroActions.style.setProperty(name, `${value}px`);
   484	            };
   485	
   486	            setPx("--hero-social-button-height", socialButtonHeight);
   487	            setPx("--hero-social-font-size", socialButtonHeight * 0.295833);
   488	            setPx("--hero-social-icon-size", socialButtonHeight * 0.672);
   489	            setPx("--hero-social-gap", socialButtonHeight * 0.045833);
   490	            setPx("--hero-social-pad-x", socialButtonHeight / 8);
   491	            setPx("--hero-view-label-font-size", socialButtonHeight * 0.275);
   492	            heroCopy?.style.setProperty(
   493	              "--hero-eyebrow-font-size",
   494	              `${socialButtonHeight * 0.367}px`,
   495	            );
   496	            heroCopy?.style.setProperty(
   497	              "--hero-lede-font-size",
   498	              `${socialButtonHeight * 0.5}px`,
   499	            );
   500	            setPx(
   501	              "--hero-carousel-base-font-size",
   502	              socialButtonHeight * 0.34375,
   503	            );
   504	            setPx(
   505	              "--hero-carousel-name-font-size",
   506	              socialButtonHeight * 0.352917,
   507	            );
   508	            setPx(
   509	              "--hero-carousel-category-font-size",
   510	              socialButtonHeight * 0.176458,
   511	            );
   512	            setPx(
   513	              "--hero-carousel-arrow-font-size",
   514	              socialButtonHeight * 0.458333,
   515	            );
   516	          }
   517	        }
   518	
   519	        window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent("hero-stack-sync"));
   520	
   521	        const viewLabel =
   522	          document.querySelector<HTMLElement>(".hero-view-label");
   523	        const githubText =
   524	          document.querySelector<HTMLElement>(".github-label-text");
   525	        const githubIcon =
   526	          document.querySelector<SVGSVGElement>(".github-icon-mark");
   527	
   528	        if (viewLabel && githubText && githubIcon) {
   529	          const viewLabelRect = viewLabel.getBoundingClientRect();
   530	          const githubTextRect = githubText.getBoundingClientRect();
   531	          const githubIconRect = githubIcon.getBoundingClientRect();
   532	          const stackLeft = githubTextRect.left - viewLabelRect.left;
   533	          const stackWidth = githubIconRect.right - githubTextRect.left;
   534	
   535	          viewLabel.style.setProperty(
   536	            "--hero-view-stack-left",
   537	            `${stackLeft}px`,
   538	          );
   539	          viewLabel.style.setProperty(
   540	            "--hero-view-stack-width",
   541	            `${stackWidth}px`,
   542	          );
   543	        }
   544	      });
   545	    };
   546	
   547	    syncHeroActionGeometry();
   548	    window.addEventListener("resize", syncHeroActionGeometry);
   549	
   550	    const targetIcon =
   551	      document.querySelector<SVGSVGElement>(".dribbble-icon-mark") ??
   552	      document.querySelector<SVGSVGElement>(".linkedin-icon-mark");
   553	    const heroActions = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>(".hero-actions");
   554	    const stackRow = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>(".stack-row");
   555	    const proofPanel = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>(".proof-panel");
   556	    const profilePhoto = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>(".profile-photo");
   557	    const targetButton = targetIcon?.closest(".hero-social-button");
   558	    const viewLabel = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>(".hero-view-label");
   559	    const githubText = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>(".github-label-text");
   560	    const githubIcon =
   561	      document.querySelector<SVGSVGElement>(".github-icon-mark");
   562	    const githubButton = githubText?.closest(".github-button");
   563	    const resizeObserver =
   564	      typeof ResizeObserver === "undefined"
   565	        ? null
   566	        : new ResizeObserver(syncHeroActionGeometry);
   567	
   568	    if (resizeObserver) {
   569	      if (projectButtonRef.current) {
   570	        resizeObserver.observe(projectButtonRef.current);
   571	      }
   572	
   573	      if (heroActions) {
   574	        resizeObserver.observe(heroActions);
   575	      }
   576	
   577	      if (stackRow) {
   578	        resizeObserver.observe(stackRow);
   579	      }
   580	
   581	      if (proofPanel) {
   582	        resizeObserver.observe(proofPanel);
   583	      }
   584	
   585	      if (profilePhoto) {
   586	        resizeObserver.observe(profilePhoto);
   587	      }
   588	
   589	      if (targetIcon) {
   590	        resizeObserver.observe(targetIcon);
   591	      }
   592	
   593	      if (targetButton) {
   594	        resizeObserver.observe(targetButton);
   595	      }
   596	
   597	      if (viewLabel) {
   598	        resizeObserver.observe(viewLabel);
   599	      }
   600	
   601	      if (githubText) {
   602	        resizeObserver.observe(githubText);
   603	      }
   604	
   605	      if (githubIcon) {
   606	        resizeObserver.observe(githubIcon);
   607	      }
   608	
   609	      if (githubButton) {
   610	        resizeObserver.observe(githubButton);
   611	      }
   612	    }
   613	
   614	    if ("fonts" in document) {
   615	      document.fonts.ready.then(syncHeroActionGeometry).catch(() => {});
   616	    }
   617	
   618	    return () => {
   619	      if (frame) {
   620	        window.cancelAnimationFrame(frame);
   621	      }
   622	
   623	      window.removeEventListener("resize", syncHeroActionGeometry);
   624	      resizeObserver?.disconnect();
   625	    };
   626	  }, []);
   627	
   628	  return (
   629	    <span className="carousel-button-group">
   630	      <a
   631	        aria-label={`Open ${activeProject.name} project`}
   632	        className="button button-primary carousel-button"
   633	        href={activeProject.href}
   634	        ref={projectButtonRef}
   635	      >
   636	        <span className="carousel-button-window" aria-live="polite">
   637	          <span className="carousel-button-label" key={activeProject.href}>
   638	            <span
   639	              className={`carousel-button-action carousel-button-action-${activeProject.tone}`}
   640	              style={{
   641	                ...strokedWhiteTextStyle,
   642	                alignItems: "center",
   643	                color: projectNameColors[activeProject.tone],
   644	                display: "inline-flex",
   645	                flexDirection: "column",
   646	                fontSize: "var(--hero-carousel-name-font-size)",
   647	                gap: "2.2px",
   648	                justifyContent: "center",
   649	                lineHeight: 0.95,
   650	              }}
   651	            >
   652	              <span
   653	                className="carousel-button-action-name"
   654	                style={{ fontSize: activeProject.nameFontSize }}
   655	              >
   656	                {activeProject.name}
   657	              </span>
   658	              <span
   659	                className="carousel-button-action-category"
   660	                style={{
   661	                  WebkitTextStroke: 0,
   662	                  color: "#000",
   663	                  fontSize: "var(--hero-carousel-category-font-size)",
   664	                  fontWeight: 900,
   665	                  letterSpacing: "0.06em",
   666	                  lineHeight: 1,
   667	                  textAlign: "center",
   668	                  textShadow: "none",
   669	                }}
   670	              >
   671	                {activeProject.category}
   672	              </span>
   673	            </span>
   674	            <ProjectDeviceStack
   675	              color={projectNameColors[activeProject.tone]}
   676	              hasTablet={activeProject.hasTablet}
   677	              hasWeb={activeProject.hasWeb}
   678	              mobilePlatforms={activeProject.mobilePlatforms}
   679	            />
   680	          </span>
   681	        </span>
   682	      </a>
   683	      <a
   684	        aria-label={`Scroll to ${activeProject.name} case study`}
   685	        className="button button-primary carousel-arrow-button"
   686	        href={`#${activeProject.caseStudyId}`}
   687	        onClick={handleArrowClick}
   688	      >
   689	        <span aria-hidden className="carousel-button-arrow">
   690	          <CarouselArrowMark />
   691	        </span>
   692	      </a>
   693	    </span>
   694	  );
   695	}

============================================================
FILE: README.md
============================================================

     1	# Prahl.dev Portfolio Site
     2	
     3	Next.js + Tailwind CSS portfolio start page for Prahl.dev.
     4	
     5	## What is included
     6	
     7	- `app/page.tsx` - the homepage/start page.
     8	- `app/globals.css` - the green/black visual system and responsive layout.
     9	- `public/images/profile-placeholder.png` - generated AI profile placeholder; replace this with your own square photo later using the same filename.
    10	- `public/images/start-page-mockup-reference.png` - the original generated mockup reference.
    11	- `public/favicon.svg` - simple green/black monogram favicon.
    12	
    13	## Local development
    14	
    15	```sh
    16	npm install
    17	npm run dev
    18	```
    19	
    20	Open `http://localhost:3000`.
    21	
    22	## Production build
    23	
    24	For Vercel, Netlify, or another Next.js host:
    25	
    26	```sh
    27	npm run build
    28	```
    29	
    30	For a simple static host:
    31	
    32	```sh
    33	npm run build:static
    34	```
    35	
    36	Then upload the generated `out/` folder.
    37	
    38	## Replace the profile photo
    39	
    40	Put your real square profile photo at:
    41	
    42	```txt
    43	public/images/profile-placeholder.png
    44	```
    45	
    46	Keep the filename the same and rebuild.


============================================================
FILE: DEPLOYMENT.md
============================================================

     1	# Deployment Notes
     2	
     3	## Best Option: Vercel
     4	
     5	1. Upload this `portfolio-site` folder to a GitHub repo.
     6	2. Import the repo in Vercel.
     7	3. Use the default Next.js settings.
     8	4. Build command: `npm run build`.
     9	
    10	## Netlify
    11	
    12	1. Upload this folder to a GitHub repo.
    13	2. Connect the repo in Netlify.
    14	3. Build command: `npm run build`.
    15	4. Publish directory: `.next`.
    16	5. Enable Netlify's Next.js runtime if prompted.
    17	
    18	## Simple Static Hosting
    19	
    20	Use this when the host only accepts HTML/CSS/JS files:
    21	
    22	```sh
    23	npm install
    24	npm run build:static
    25	```
    26	
    27	Upload the contents of:
    28	
    29	```txt
    30	out/
    31	```
    32	
    33	This mode does not need a running Node.js server after upload.
    34	
    35	## Contact Button
    36	
    37	The contact button currently uses:
    38	
    39	```txt
    40	mailto:hello@example.com
    41	```
    42	
    43	Replace `hello@example.com` in `app/page.tsx` with your real email address.

============================================================
FILE: .github/workflows/hostinger-static-export.yml
============================================================

     1	name: Build static export for Hostinger
     2	
     3	on:
     4	  push:
     5	    branches: [main]
     6	  workflow_dispatch:
     7	
     8	permissions:
     9	  contents: write
    10	
    11	concurrency:
    12	  group: hostinger-static-export
    13	  cancel-in-progress: true
    14	
    15	jobs:
    16	  build-and-publish:
    17	    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    18	    steps:
    19	      - name: Check out source
    20	        uses: actions/checkout@v4
    21	
    22	      - name: Set up Node
    23	        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
    24	        with:
    25	          node-version: 22
    26	          cache: npm
    27	
    28	      - name: Install dependencies
    29	        run: npm ci
    30	
    31	      - name: Build static export
    32	        run: npm run build:static
    33	
    34	      - name: Publish static export branch
    35	        env:
    36	          GITHUB_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
    37	        run: |
    38	          cd out
    39	          git init -b hostinger-deploy
    40	          git config user.name "github-actions[bot]"
    41	          git config user.email "41898282+github-actions[bot]@users.noreply.github.com"
    42	          git add -A
    43	          git commit -m "Deploy static export from ${GITHUB_SHA}"
    44	          git remote add origin "https://x-access-token:${GITHUB_TOKEN}@github.com/${GITHUB_REPOSITORY}.git"
    45	          git push --force origin hostinger-deploy

============================================================
FILE: read_project.sh
============================================================

     1	#!/bin/bash
     2	
     3	PROJECT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "$0")" && pwd)"
     4	OUTPUT_FILE="$PROJECT_DIR/portfolio_PROJECT_SNAPSHOT.txt"
     5	
     6	echo "Generating Portfolio project snapshot..."
     7	echo "Project directory: $PROJECT_DIR"
     8	echo "Snapshot: $OUTPUT_FILE"
     9	echo ""
    10	
    11	write_header() {
    12	  cat > "$OUTPUT_FILE" <<EOF
    13	Portfolio Next.js PROJECT SNAPSHOT
    14	Generated: $(date)
    15	Project directory: $PROJECT_DIR
    16	
    17	IMPORTANT INSTRUCTIONS FOR CHATGPT & CODEX:
    18	1. Read this entire snapshot before giving code edits.
    19	2. Preserve all assets, spacing, alignment, fonts, images, layout, animations, and relative positioning unless specifically asked to change them.
    20	3. Do not remove unrelated code.
    21	4. Do not rewrite large sections unless requested.
    22	5. When giving code changes, include exact line/row numbers whenever possible.
    23	6. Print full scripts when requested.
    24	7. Treat this project structure as the source of truth.
    25	8. If you do not understand something, ask for clarification instead of making assumptions.
    26	9. Warn me, or at least caution me, if I ask for something that would break the project or cause it to not work as intended.
    27	10. For this Portfolio repo/website project, always ask me for the commit message before committing or pushing.
    28	
    29	
    30	============================================================
    31	PORTFOLIO PROJECT NOTES
    32	============================================================
    33	
    34	- Main source branch: main
    35	- Deployment source: GitHub Actions builds main into the hostinger-deploy branch
    36	- Hostinger root directory: public_html
    37	- Main stack represented by the website: React / React Native, Next.js, Tailwind CSS, Node.js, Kotlin
    38	- Public website assets live under public/
    39	- Run this script before starting a Portfolio session to refresh the project snapshot.
    40	
    41	
    42	============================================================
    43	SNAPSHOT IGNORE POLICY
    44	============================================================
    45	
    46	This file is rebuilt from the current Portfolio workspace every time ./read_project.sh runs.
    47	Ignored paths are omitted from the project tree and file dumps unless they appear inside an included text file such as .gitignore or read_project.sh.
    48	
    49	The snapshot intentionally ignores generated/cache/runtime/private files:
    50	- .git
    51	- node_modules
    52	- .next
    53	- out
    54	- dist
    55	- build
    56	- .cache
    57	- .turbo
    58	- .npm
    59	- .pnpm-store
    60	- .yarn
    61	- .DS_Store
    62	- next-env.d.ts
    63	- *.tsbuildinfo
    64	- *_PROJECT_SNAPSHOT.txt
    65	- *.zip
    66	- .env and .env*.local
    67	
    68	Binary image, PDF, and archive files are inventoried by path, size, and modified time only. Raw binary bytes are not printed.
    69	
    70	
    71	============================================================
    72	PROJECT FILE TREE
    73	============================================================
    74	
    75	EOF
    76	}
    77	
    78	print_file() {
    79	  local file="$1"
    80	
    81	  if [ -f "$file" ]; then
    82	    {
    83	      echo ""
    84	      echo ""
    85	      echo "============================================================"
    86	      echo "FILE: ${file#$PROJECT_DIR/}"
    87	      echo "============================================================"
    88	      echo ""
    89	      nl -ba "$file"
    90	    } >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    91	  fi
    92	}
    93	
    94	print_inventory_header() {
    95	  local title="$1"
    96	
    97	  {
    98	    echo ""
    99	    echo ""
   100	    echo "============================================================"
   101	    echo "$title"
   102	    echo "============================================================"
   103	    echo ""
   104	  } >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
   105	}
   106	
   107	print_file_inventory_line() {
   108	  local file="$1"
   109	  local size
   110	  local modified
   111	
   112	  size="$(stat -f "%z" "$file" 2>/dev/null || stat -c "%s" "$file" 2>/dev/null || echo "unknown")"
   113	  modified="$(stat -f "%Sm" -t "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S" "$file" 2>/dev/null || stat -c "%y" "$file" 2>/dev/null || echo "unknown")"
   114	  printf '%s | %s bytes | modified %s\n' "${file#$PROJECT_DIR/}" "$size" "$modified" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
   115	}
   116	
   117	print_dir_inventory() {
   118	  local title="$1"
   119	  local dir="$2"
   120	
   121	  print_inventory_header "$title"
   122	
   123	  if [ ! -d "$dir" ]; then
   124	    echo "Directory not present: ${dir#$PROJECT_DIR/}" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
   125	    return
   126	  fi
   127	
   128	  find "$dir" -type f \
   129	    ! -name ".DS_Store" \
   130	    ! -name "*_PROJECT_SNAPSHOT.txt" \
   131	    | sort | while IFS= read -r file; do
   132	    print_file_inventory_line "$file"
   133	  done
   134	}
   135	
   136	print_matching_inventory() {
   137	  local title="$1"
   138	  shift
   139	
   140	  print_inventory_header "$title"
   141	
   142	  find "$PROJECT_DIR" "$@" -type f \
   143	    ! -path "$PROJECT_DIR/.git/*" \
   144	    ! -path "$PROJECT_DIR/node_modules/*" \
   145	    ! -path "$PROJECT_DIR/.next/*" \
   146	    ! -path "$PROJECT_DIR/out/*" \
   147	    ! -name ".DS_Store" \
   148	    ! -name "*_PROJECT_SNAPSHOT.txt" \
   149	    | sort | while IFS= read -r file; do
   150	    print_file_inventory_line "$file"
   151	  done
   152	}
   153	
   154	append_git_context() {
   155	  {
   156	    echo ""
   157	    echo ""
   158	    echo "============================================================"
   159	    echo "GIT CONTEXT"
   160	    echo "============================================================"
   161	    echo ""
   162	    echo "Current branch:"
   163	    git -C "$PROJECT_DIR" branch --show-current 2>/dev/null || true
   164	    echo ""
   165	    echo "Status:"
   166	    git -C "$PROJECT_DIR" status --short --branch 2>/dev/null || true
   167	    echo ""
   168	    echo "Recent commits:"
   169	    git -C "$PROJECT_DIR" log --oneline --decorate -10 2>/dev/null || true
   170	    echo ""
   171	    echo "Remotes:"
   172	    git -C "$PROJECT_DIR" remote -v 2>/dev/null || true
   173	  } >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
   174	}
   175	
   176	write_snapshot() {
   177	  write_header
   178	
   179	  find "$PROJECT_DIR" \
   180	    -path "$PROJECT_DIR/.git" -prune -o \
   181	    -path "$PROJECT_DIR/node_modules" -prune -o \
   182	    -path "$PROJECT_DIR/.next" -prune -o \
   183	    -path "$PROJECT_DIR/out" -prune -o \
   184	    -path "$PROJECT_DIR/dist" -prune -o \
   185	    -path "$PROJECT_DIR/build" -prune -o \
   186	    -path "$PROJECT_DIR/.cache" -prune -o \
   187	    -path "$PROJECT_DIR/.turbo" -prune -o \
   188	    -path "$PROJECT_DIR/.npm" -prune -o \
   189	    -path "$PROJECT_DIR/.pnpm-store" -prune -o \
   190	    -path "$PROJECT_DIR/.yarn" -prune -o \
   191	    -name ".DS_Store" -prune -o \
   192	    -name "next-env.d.ts" -prune -o \
   193	    -name "*.tsbuildinfo" -prune -o \
   194	    -name "*_PROJECT_SNAPSHOT.txt" -prune -o \
   195	    -name "*.zip" -prune -o \

   239	  do

   241	  done
   242

   246	  print_matching_inventory "PDF WORKLOG INVENTORY" \( -name "portfolio_worklog_*.pdf" \)
   247	  print_matching_inventory "DEPLOYMENT ARCHIVE INVENTORY" \( -name "*.zip" \)
   248

- .git
- node_modules
- .next
- out
- dist
- build
- .cache
- .turbo
- .npm
- .pnpm-store
- .yarn
- .DS_Store

- *.tsbuildinfo
- *_PROJECT_SNAPSHOT.txt
- *.zip

The snapshot lists public images, PDF worklogs, and deployment archives by path, size, and modified time, but does not print raw PNG/JPG/PDF/ZIP bytes.
